(function (window) {
  function jw() {
    this._functions = [];
    this.run = function (func) {
      this._functions.push(func);
    };
    this.resolve = function (arg) {
      this.run = function (func) {
        func(arg);
      };
      for (var i = 0; i < this._functions.length; i++) {
        var func = this._functions[i];
        delete this._functions[i];
        func(arg);
      }
    };
  }
  var rqw = new jw();

  window.rqw = function (fnc) {
    rqw.run(fnc);
  };
  window.rqw.resolve = function () {
    return rqw.resolve.apply(rqw, arguments);
  };

<script>
    var reloadable_banners = {};

    function reload_banners(){
        try{
            if(!document.hidden){
                for (let banner_id in reloadable_banners){
                    let banner_element = document.getElementById(banner_id);
                    if(!!banner_element){
                        let b = banner_element.getBoundingClientRect();
                        if( (b.top+b.height/2)>0 && (b.top+b.height/2)<window.innerHeight){
                            window.reloadable_banners[banner_id] += 1;
                            if(window.reloadable_banners[banner_id]==7){
                                // window.reloadable_banners[banner_id] = 0;
                                banner_element.style.minHeight = b.height+"px";
                                Ya.adfoxCode.reload(banner_id);
                                try{
                                    ym(8092381,'reachGoal','ad_reload',{ 'ad_reload': banner_id });
                                }catch(e){}
                            }
                        }
                    };
                };
            };
            // console.log( reloadable_banners );
        }catch(e){}
    };

    setInterval(reload_banners, 5000);


    function AdFox_banner_create(containerId, banner_params, w, n, lazy=false){
        
            var params = banner_params;
    
            params.p2 = params.p2 || 'hhvm';
            params.pp = params.pp || (w.innerWidth >= 336 ? 'bqzc':'bqzd');
            params.ps = params.ps || 'crea';

            try{var info1 = w.page_tag_info;}catch(e){}
            
            var ad_keys = '';
            try{ad_keys += ' n'+w.Drupal.settings.site.nid;}catch(e){}
            try{ad_keys += ' n'+info1.prod_id;}catch(e){}
            try{ad_keys += ' t'+info1.tags.join(' t');}catch(e){}
            try{ad_keys += ' t'+info1.category_tids.join(' t');}catch(e){}
        
            try{if(!!info1.type_id){ ad_keys += ' t'+info1.type_id;}}catch(e){}
            try{if(!!info1.brand_id){ ad_keys += ' t'+info1.brand_id;}}catch(e){}
        
            try{
                params['pk'] = ad_keys;
                params['pke'] = 1;
            }catch(e){}
        
            try{params['puid1'] = info1.tags.join(':');}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid2'] = info1.prod_id;}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid3'] = w.Drupal.settings.site.type;}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid4'] = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid5'] = w.Drupal.settings.site.uid != 0 }catch(e){}
            try{params['puid6'] = (info1.gavgav === 'gavgav'+'_0') ? 'no' : 'yes'; }catch(e){}
        
            try{
                params['puid7'] = w.ab_var;
            }catch(e){}
    


            try{
                if(!!w.ab_test){
                    params['puid8'] = w.ab_test;
                    // params['puid8'] = w.adfox_admanager_test;
                    params['partner-stat-id'] = params['puid8'];
                }
            }catch(e){}
    

            if(lazy){
                w.yaContextCb.push(()=>{
                    Ya.adfoxCode.createScroll({
                        ownerId: 265680,
                        containerId: containerId,
                        params: params,
                        lazyLoad: {
                            fetchMargin: 200,
                            mobileScaling: 2,
                        },
                        onRender: function() { try{ window.reloadable_banners[containerId] = document.getElementById(containerId).classList.contains("NOREFRESH")?-100:0; }catch(e){} }
                    })
                });
            }else{
                w.yaContextCb.push(()=>{
                    Ya.adfoxCode.create({
                        ownerId: 265680,
                        containerId: containerId,
                        params: params,
                        onRender: function() { try{ window.reloadable_banners[containerId] = document.getElementById(containerId).classList.contains("NOREFRESH")?-100:0; }catch(e){} }
                    })
                });
                // console.log(params);
            }
        
    }
        
        
    function ADX_banner_create(containerId, adx_ad_slot, adx_container_style, w, data_ad_client='ca-pub-8313361070310510', auto_responsive=false ){
    
            try {
                if(w.page_tag_info.gavgav === 'gavgav_0'){    
                    // var adx_div_container = w.document.getElementById(containerId);
                    // adx_div_container.innerHTML = '<ins class="adsbygoogle"      style="' + adx_container_style + '"      data-ad-client="ca-pub-8313361070310510"      data-ad-slot="' + adx_ad_slot + '"></ins>';
    
                    var ins   = document.createElement("ins");
                    ins.setAttribute('class','adsbygoogle');
                    ins.setAttribute('style', adx_container_style);
                    ins.setAttribute('data-ad-client', data_ad_client);
                    ins.setAttribute('data-ad-slot', adx_ad_slot);
                    
                    if(auto_responsive){
                        ins.setAttribute('data-ad-format','auto');
                        ins.setAttribute('data-full-width-responsive','true');
                    }
    
                    w.document.getElementById(containerId).appendChild(ins);                
    
                    (w.adsbygoogle = w.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
                }
            } catch (e) {};
        
    }
    
    
    
    
    
    

    
    
    
    </script>

<script>

  jqw(function ($) {
    try {
      if (Adapt && (Adapt.getCurrentState() == 'min'  ||  Adapt.getCurrentState() == 'middle') )     {
        return;
      }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    var f = function () {
      try {
        var si = $('#sidebar > .sidebar-inset-wrapper');
        var rt = 0;
        if ($('#sidebar-right-top').length > 0) {
          rt = $('#sidebar-right-top').height();
        }

        var mh = ($('#content').height() - rt) - 10;
        //console.log('tt', mh)
        si.css('min-height', mh);
      } catch (e) {
      }
    };
    f();
    setInterval(f, 1300);
  });

</script>

            let cls = 0;
            let cls_01 = false;
            let cls_025 = false;

            new PerformanceObserver((entryList) => {
